import numpy as np
9
import scipy.linalg
10
11
def CalculateVbusMin(Xgen, delta_deviation , Py, Ly, Uy, busNumbers ,
busNumbers_dyn , ngens, CM_index, Pgenrou, Pgensal ,nbus, GDMVA,
genroubusIndex , gensalbusIndex ,Sbase, t):
12
13
delta_dr = delta_deviation
14
15
rotate_delta = np.zeros(ngens)
16
17
rotate_delta[CM_index] = delta_dr
18
19
rotate_delta_genrou = rotate_delta[genroubusIndex]
20
rotate_delta_gensal = rotate_delta[gensalbusIndex]
21
22
# Initializing Ig
23
Ig = np.zeros(nbus, dtype=np.complex)
24
Igen = np.zeros(ngens, dtype=np.complex)
25
26
if Pgensal is not None:
27
Xgensal = Xgen[1]
28
29
delta = Xgensal[0]
30
omega = Xgensal[1]
31
Psiq_subtr = Xgensal[4]
32
Psid_tr = Xgensal[3]
33
Eq_tr = Xgensal[2]
34
Xd_tr = Pgensal[2]
35
Xd_subtr = Pgensal[3]
36
Xl = Pgensal[4]
37
38
Psid_subtr = Eq_tr * (Xd_subtr - Xl) / (Xd_tr - Xl) + Psid_tr *
(Xd_tr - Xd_subtr) / (Xd_tr - Xl)
39
40
E = (-Psiq_subtr + 1j * Psid_subtr) * omega
# Calculating
internal voltage on stator
41
42
# shifting the phase of E with delta_dr:
43
E = E*np.exp(1j*rotate_delta_gensal)
==PAGE:275==
F.2 Implementation of TSA and TVSA
261
44
45
# Calculating generator current
46
I_genref = E / (1j * Xd_subtr)
# Calculating the Norton current
, using the thevenin voltage and thevenin impedance.
47
I_netref_genbase = I_genref * np.exp(1j * (delta - np.pi / 2))
48
I_netref_Sbase = I_netref_genbase * GDMVA[gensalbusIndex , 1] /
Sbase
49
50
Igen[gensalbusIndex] = I_netref_Sbase
51
52
53
if Pgenrou is not None:
54
Xgenrou = Xgen[0]
55
56
delta = Xgenrou[0]
57
omega = Xgenrou[1]
58
Eq_tr = Xgenrou[2]
59
Ed_tr = Xgenrou[3]
60
Psiq_tr = Xgenrou[4]
61
Psid_tr = Xgenrou[5]
62
63
Xd_tr = Pgenrou[2]
64
Xq_tr = Pgenrou[3]
65
Xd_subtr = Pgenrou[4]
66
Xl = Pgenrou[5]
67
68
Psiq_subtr = -(Ed_tr * (Xd_subtr - Xl) / (Xq_tr - Xl) + Psiq_tr
* (Xq_tr - Xd_subtr) / (Xq_tr - Xl))
69
Psid_subtr = Eq_tr * (Xd_subtr - Xl) / (Xd_tr - Xl) + Psid_tr *
(Xd_tr - Xd_subtr) / (Xd_tr - Xl)
70
71
E = (-Psiq_subtr + 1j * Psid_subtr) * omega
# internal voltage
on stator side
72
73
# shifting the phase of E with delta_dr:
74
E = E*np.exp(1j*rotate_delta_genrou)
75
76
# Calculating generator current
77
I_genref = E / (1j * Xd_subtr)
78
I_netref_genbase = I_genref * np.exp(1j * (delta - np.pi / 2))
79
I_netref_Sbase = I_netref_genbase * GDMVA[genroubusIndex , 1] /
Sbase
80
81
Igen[genroubusIndex] = I_netref_Sbase
82
83
84
# Igen is ordered according to busNumbers_dyn
85
# The generator currents from Igen has to be stored at the correct
indexes in Ig to match the correct generator.
86
# Ig is ordered according to busNumbers , and hence contains a
current injection at each bus in the system.
87
for i, busName in enumerate(busNumbers):
==PAGE:276==
F.3 Real-time implementation with WARTApp
262
88
ind = np.where(busNumbers_dyn == busName)[0]
# gives the index
where busName is located in busNumbers_dyn
89
if np.size(ind) == 0:
90
continue
91
else:
92
if len(ind) == 1:
93
ind = ind[0]
94
Ig[i] = Igen[ind]
95
96
elif len(ind) > 1:
97
for IND in ind:
98
Ig[i] += Igen[IND]
# adding the two generator
currents to find the total current injected into
the bus
99
100
Ig = np.transpose(np.array([Ig]))
101
102
# Updating the system voltages, U at each bus in the system
103
104
U = (scipy.linalg.inv(Py @ Ly @ Uy) @ Ig).reshape(1, -1)[0]
105
106
return U

def LocateTransientVoltagSags(self,VbusMinActualLoadbuses ,
VbusMinIndexes ,dV_load_buses ,time,time_stop_fault): #
VbusMinIndexes contains indexes of load buses which are below
0.7 p.u.
==PAGE:280==
F.3 Real-time implementation with WARTApp
266
136
137
if VbusMinIndexes.any() == True:
138
139
VbusMinValue = VbusMinActualLoadbuses[VbusMinIndexes]
140
141
# load buses where the voltage is < 0.7 (value and bus name)
:
142
# extracting contribution from each generator for the load
buses where a transient voltage sag is occurring.
143
dV_critical_load_buses_gen_contribution = dV_load_buses[
VbusMinIndexes , :] # dV_load_buses is a nload x ngen
matrix containing the voltage change contribution to
each load bus for each generator
144
critical_load_bus_name = self.ld.busNumbers[self.ld.
Zloadindexes[VbusMinIndexes]].astype(np.int)
145
146
# generator contributing most negative in reducing the
voltage (value and bus name):
147
largest_load_voltage_decrease = np.min(
dV_critical_load_buses_gen_contribution , axis=1) # the
value which decreases the load buses voltage with the
most, which comes from the critical generator
148
total_load_voltage_decrease = np.sum(
dV_critical_load_buses_gen_contribution , axis=1)
149
critical_generator_names = self.ldyn.busNumbers_dyn[np.
argmin(dV_critical_load_buses_gen_contribution , axis=1)
].astype(np.int)
150
critical_generator_id = np.array(self.ld.Generators['Id'][np
.argmin(dV_critical_load_buses_gen_contribution , axis=1)
],dtype=np.int)
151
152
TransientVoltageSagData = [VbusMinValue ,
critical_load_bus_name ,largest_load_voltage_decrease ,
total_load_voltage_decrease ,critical_generator_names ,
critical_generator_id ,time,time-time_stop_fault]
153
154
return TransientVoltageSagData

def ExtractTrueMinimum(self,Vabs_loads ,Time,time_stop_fault): # only
used for the sensitivity analysis to locate the true minimum
voltage and the time it occurs
158
159
stop_fault_ind = np.where(Time == time_stop_fault)[0][1] #
taking the t+ value where the voltages have recovered after
the fault
160
161
Vabs_loads_min = Vabs_loads[np.arange(stop_fault_ind ,len(
Vabs_loads[:,0]))].min(axis=0) # finding the minimum voltage
after the fault clearance
162
163
Vabs_loads_min_ind = Vabs_loads_min <= 0.7
==PAGE:281==
F.3 Real-time implementation with WARTApp
267
164
165
if Vabs_loads_min_ind.any() == True:
166
167
Vabs_loads_min = Vabs_loads_min[Vabs_loads_min_ind]
168
169
T_Vmin_ind = Vabs_loads[np.arange(stop_fault_ind ,len(
Vabs_loads[:,0]))].argmin(axis=0)+stop_fault_ind #
finding the index after fault clearance where the
minimum occurs
170
T_Vmin_ind = T_Vmin_ind[Vabs_loads_min_ind]
171
172
time_Vmin = Time[T_Vmin_ind] # finding the time after fault
clearance where the minimum occurs
173
174
load_bus_name = self.ld.busNumbers[self.ld.Zloadindexes[
Vabs_loads_min_ind]].astype(np.int)
175
176
TransientVoltageSagData = [Vabs_loads_min ,time_Vmin,
load_bus_name]
177
178
return TransientVoltageSagData

'''
2
3
Screening mechanism which screens through each contingency.
4
5
Ensure the correct path for the raw and dyr-file is set.
6
7
This file supports both online and offline usage.
8
9
Online: Real-time assessment by coupling it with WARTApp.
10
Offline: Run this file as the main, provide a RAW and DYR file located
on the local PC.
11
12
VminValue is used to control which minimums the screening mechanism
needs to save.
13
